        <div class="entry box isotope-item">
         <div class="entry-intro">
          <h1>
           10 Scientists who Were Killed by Their Own Experiments
          </h1>
         </div>
         <div class="post-body">
          <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="360" src="http://videochart.net/framevideo/71354.7825ba6e727bb6414ef11346497c?width=580&amp;height=360" width="580">
          </iframe>
          <script async="" src="//pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js">
          </script>
          <!-- The Amazing Stuff Resposive New -->
          <ins class="adsbygoogle" data-ad-client="ca-pub-6418595111181168" data-ad-format="auto" data-ad-slot="9284855290" style="display:block">
          </ins>
          <script>
           (adsbygoogle = window.adsbygoogle || []).push({});
          </script>
          <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
          </div>
          <div style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          </div>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
            <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_d2hhrNRmcKw/TOA-vVY-9WI/AAAAAAAABAI/BgHbBaZsjBo/s1600/Galileo-Galilei.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
             <img border="0" height="400" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_d2hhrNRmcKw/TOA-vVY-9WI/AAAAAAAABAI/BgHbBaZsjBo/s400/Galileo-Galilei.jpg" width="323"/>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           <br/>
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           <br/>
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           These are the great people whose discoveries have changed the world but they were unfortunate as they died or injured themselves while performing their experiments.The advances they have made to science are incredible and many of them opened the doors for some of mans greatest discoveries andinventions.
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           <br/>
          </div>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
          </h3>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
          </h3>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           1. Sir David Brewster
          </h3>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif; text-align: center;">
           <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
            <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_d2hhrNRmcKw/TOA-t6uXtOI/AAAAAAAABAA/kUWVhfb6Tpg/s1600/David-Brewster.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
             <img border="0" height="640" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_d2hhrNRmcKw/TOA-t6uXtOI/AAAAAAAABAA/kUWVhfb6Tpg/s640/David-Brewster.jpg" width="465"/>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           <br/>
           Sir David was a Scottish scientist, and a writer. Optics and light polarization was the field of his interest. Optics is aa field requiring excellent vision. In 1831, Sir David performed a chemical experiment which almostblinded him. He remained affected with eye troubles until his death. Sir David Brewster is well known asthe inventor of the kaleidoscope  a toy that has gives joy to millions of children over theyears.
          </div>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
          </h3>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
          </h3>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           2. Alexander Bogdanov
          </h3>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif; text-align: center;">
           <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
            <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_d2hhrNRmcKw/TOA-tA1_SFI/AAAAAAAAA_8/lUIchZUNQME/s1600/Alexander-Bogdanov.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
             <img border="0" height="640" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_d2hhrNRmcKw/TOA-tA1_SFI/AAAAAAAAA_8/lUIchZUNQME/s640/Alexander-Bogdanov.jpg" width="436"/>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           <br/>
           Alexander Bogdanov was a Russian physician, philosopher, economist, and a science fiction writer. In 1924, hestarted experiments with blood transfusion. After performing 11 transfusionshimself, he stated that he had suspended his balding, and improved his eyesight. Unfortunately, Bogdanov forgot to test the health of the blood of the donor which he was using. In 1928, Bogdanov took a transfusion of blood infected with malaria and tuberculosis which madehim died shortly.
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           <br/>
          </div>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
          </h3>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
          </h3>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           3. Karl Scheele
          </h3>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif; text-align: center;">
           <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
            <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_d2hhrNRmcKw/TOA-xtd_osI/AAAAAAAABAU/Inf1H883ujo/s1600/Karl-Scheele.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
             <img border="0" height="640" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_d2hhrNRmcKw/TOA-xtd_osI/AAAAAAAABAU/Inf1H883ujo/s640/Karl-Scheele.jpg" width="490"/>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           <br/>
           Scheele was a pharmaceutical chemist and had discovered many chemical elements. The most notable of his discoveries were oxygen,molybdenum, tungsten, manganese and chlorine. He also discovered a process very similar to pasteurization.Scheele had the habit of taste testing his discoveries and managed to survive his taste-test of hydrogen cyanide. But he was unfortunate while tasting mercury and died from the symptoms of mercury poisoning.
          </div>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
          </h3>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
          </h3>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           4. Elizabeth Ascheim
          </h3>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif; text-align: center;">
           <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
            <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_d2hhrNRmcKw/TOA-utOQkeI/AAAAAAAABAE/3JC82YISTzY/s1600/Elizabeth-Ascheim.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
             <img border="0" height="640" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_d2hhrNRmcKw/TOA-utOQkeI/AAAAAAAABAE/3JC82YISTzY/s640/Elizabeth-Ascheim.jpg" width="460"/>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           <br/>
           After the death of the mother, Elizabeth Fleischman Ascheim married her family doctor, Woolf. Woolf was very much exited about the new discovery of Wilhelm Conrad Rntgen x-rays. His wife alsobecame equally interested in it and she gave up her job as a bookkeeper tocontinuestudies in electrical science. Finally, she bought an x-ray machine and kept it in her husbands office which was the first x-ray lab in San Francisco.
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           Using themselves as subjects,She and her husband spent some years in experimenting with the machine. Unfortunately, they did not realize the consequences of theirlack of protection to x-rays and Elizabeth died of an extremely widespread and violent cancer.
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           <br/>
          </div>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
          </h3>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
          </h3>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           5. Jean Francois De Rozier
          </h3>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif; text-align: center;">
           <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
            <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_d2hhrNRmcKw/TOA-w5PNg3I/AAAAAAAABAQ/qWZSE7rTWJg/s1600/Jean-Francois-De-Rozier.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
             <img border="0" height="640" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_d2hhrNRmcKw/TOA-w5PNg3I/AAAAAAAABAQ/qWZSE7rTWJg/s640/Jean-Francois-De-Rozier.jpg" width="438"/>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           <br/>
           Jean Francois was a teacher of chemistry and physics. In 1783, he witnessed the worlds first balloon flight that created a passion in him for flight. Aftertesting various flights of a sheep, a chicken, and a duck, he took the first manned free flight in a balloon. Hetraveledat an altitude of 3,000 feetusing a hot air balloon. Later, De Rozier planned a crossing of the English Channel from France to England. He took the flight but unfortunately after reaching 1,500 feet in a combined hot air and gas balloon, the balloon deflated and made him to fall to his death.
          </div>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
          </h3>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
          </h3>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           6. Sir Humphry Davy
          </h3>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif; text-align: center;">
           <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
            <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_d2hhrNRmcKw/TOA-wFjvFmI/AAAAAAAABAM/FxZYc93JQG8/s1600/Humphrey-Davy.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
             <img border="0" height="640" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_d2hhrNRmcKw/TOA-wFjvFmI/AAAAAAAABAM/FxZYc93JQG8/s640/Humphrey-Davy.jpg" width="507"/>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           <br/>
           Sir Humphry Davy was a brilliant British chemist and inventor. He got a very rough start to his science career. As a young trainee, he was fired from his jobbecause he caused too many explosions while performingexperiments. He was so much passionate about chemistry that he took it up as the field of his career. He had a habit of inhaling various gases whiledealing with them. Luckily this habit led to his discovery of the anesthetic properties of nitrous oxide. But, unfortunately, this same habit led to himnearly killing himself on many occasions. The frequent poisonings of gases made him useless for the remaining two decades of his life. He had alsodamaged his eyes permanentlyin a nitrogen trichloride explosion.
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           <br/>
          </div>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
          </h3>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
          </h3>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           7. Michael Faraday
          </h3>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif; text-align: center;">
           <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
            <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_d2hhrNRmcKw/TOA-0D5smII/AAAAAAAABAg/R2q5xk07ZLg/s1600/Michael-Faraday.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
             <img border="0" height="640" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_d2hhrNRmcKw/TOA-0D5smII/AAAAAAAABAg/R2q5xk07ZLg/s640/Michael-Faraday.jpg" width="494"/>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           <br/>
           After the injury of a brilliant British chemistSir Humphrey Davys eyes, Faraday became an trainee to him. He made efforts to improve Davys methods of electrolysis and tomake useful discoveries in the field of electro-magnetics. Unfortunately, Faraday also suffered damageto his eyes in a nitrogen chloride explosion. He spent the rest of his life suffering with chronic chemical poisoning.
          </div>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
          </h3>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
          </h3>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           8. Galileo Galilei
          </h3>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif; text-align: center;">
           <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
            <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_d2hhrNRmcKw/TOA-vVY-9WI/AAAAAAAABAI/BgHbBaZsjBo/s1600/Galileo-Galilei.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
             <img border="0" height="640" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_d2hhrNRmcKw/TOA-vVY-9WI/AAAAAAAABAI/BgHbBaZsjBo/s640/Galileo-Galilei.jpg" width="517"/>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           <br/>
           Galileo also referred to as the father of modern physics. Hiswork on the refinement of the telescope was brilliant. It opened up the doors of the universe for future generations. But it also damaged his eyesight. He wasfascinated with the sun and spent many hours staring at it. As a result of which, he got extreme damage to his retinas. This was the most likely cause of his near blindness in thelast four years of his life.
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           <br/>
          </div>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
          </h3>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
          </h3>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           9. Louis Slotin
          </h3>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif; text-align: center;">
           <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
            <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_d2hhrNRmcKw/TOA-yTA_8-I/AAAAAAAABAY/bYvXOsmFdAE/s1600/Louis-Slotin.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
             <img border="0" height="316" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_d2hhrNRmcKw/TOA-yTA_8-I/AAAAAAAABAY/bYvXOsmFdAE/s400/Louis-Slotin.jpg" width="400"/>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           <br/>
           Slotin worked on the US project to design the first nuclear bomb. While performing experiments for his project, he accidentallydropped a sphere of beryllium on a second sphere causing a prompt critical. It is known from other scientists who were inthe room that they had witnessed a blue glow of air ionization and felt a heat wave. Slotin was rushed to hospital where he died nine days later.
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           The amount of radiation he was exposed to was equivalent to standing 4800 feet away from an atomic bomb explosion.
          </div>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
          </h3>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
          </h3>
          <h3 style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           10. Marie Curie
          </h3>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif; text-align: center;">
           <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
            <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_d2hhrNRmcKw/TOA-zH5whYI/AAAAAAAABAc/PQd3OeRxmlk/s1600/Marie-Curie.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
             <img border="0" height="640" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_d2hhrNRmcKw/TOA-zH5whYI/AAAAAAAABAc/PQd3OeRxmlk/s640/Marie-Curie.jpg" width="434"/>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           <br/>
          </div>
          <div style="font-family: Verdana,sans-serif;">
           Curie along with her husband Pierre discovered radium in 1898. She spent rest of her life performing radiation research and studying radiation therapy.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           Her constant exposure to radiation led to her contracting leukemia and due to which she died in 1934. Curie is the first and only person who received two Nobel prizes in sciencein two different fields, chemistry and physics.
          </div>
          <div class="shareaholic-canvas" data-app="share_buttons" data-app-id="319159">
